#####

Old Phone will be rejected during pickup if

*   * Phone is not in working condition
  * RAM/Storage/IMEI do not match or verification on Rabbit Exchange App fails
  * Screen lock or icloud lock is not disabled.
  * Phone has damages on body (bends, dents, cracks, scratches, loose panel) or screen (discoloration, dead pixels, cracks, spots, lines, traces of replacement)

#####

Exchange tip

  * If old phone is rejected during pickup, you can pay the exchange discount amount at the time of delivery by card or cash and keep the new phone
  * The “Limited-Time Discount” will not be refunded if the old item is successfully picked up

##  10 days Service Centre Replacement

Replacement Reason  |  Replacement Period  |  Replacement Policy   
---|---|---  
Defective Item  |  10 days from delivery  |  iQOO warranty policy (at Service Centre)   
Physical Damage,  
Wrong and Missing Item  |  10 days from delivery  |  Replacement   
  
__

Defective item:

  * Amazon may provide support via self-help guides or on call or at doorstep, as applicable. 
  * If this issue is not resolved, please contact iQOO or visit the Service Centre.
  * iQOO will repair the product or provide a replacement or Defective certificate, as applicable. The time taken for resolution will be as per iQOO warranty policies.
  * Please check for nearest Brand service center in your location. For details [ click here ](https://www.amazon.in/gp/help/customer/display.html?ie=UTF8&nodeId=202064020)

  
Physical Damage, Wrong, Missing Items:

  * Returns will not be accepted if it is an Open Box Delivery order
  * Remote verification by image/video will be done by Amazon

[__ Know More ](javascript:void\(0\))

#  Replacement Instructions

![](https://m.media-amazon.com/images/I/11Sa2OpQXzL.png)

Keep the item in its original condition and packaging along with the MRP tag
and accessories. Unlock the device (screen lock, iCloud lock, etc.) and delete
your Google account for a successful pick-up.

#  Replacement verification

![](https://m.media-amazon.com/images/I/11aVEj4+dRL.png)

During on-call support, you may be prompted to download a diagnostic app or
upload an image for verification. Please visit the nearest iQOO Service Centre
for product-related issues. Further support will be provided by the brand at
their service centre as per their warranty policies.

#  About this item

  * Powerful Dimensity 7400 5G Processor with 750K+ AnTuTu Score* - Built on flagship 4nm TSMC process technology to provide exceptional power-efficiency. Comes with Large Graphite cooling area to give excellent heat management. 
  * India’s Slimmest Quad-Curved Display Smartphone* - Just 0.739 cm thin and stunning from every angle! Dive into a 6.77" immersive display with 120Hz refresh rate, HDR10+ clarity, and up to 1800 nits brightness. And with a massive 5700mAh battery and 44W FlashCharge, you get all-day power in this slim, stylish design. 
  * Segment-Leading 32MP 4K Selfie Camera* - Capture true-to-life 4K videos and unleash your inner director. 
  * Sony IMX882 4K OIS Rear Camera - The rear Sony main camera supports 4K ultra-clear video with hybrid (OIS + EIS) anti-shake, so you can shoot clear & highly stable videos. 
  * IP68 & IP69 Rated + Military-Grade Shock Resistance + SGS 5-star Anti Fall Protection - Engineered to withstand dust, rain, and accidental drops with industry leading durability standards. SGS & Military-grade provide excellent protection from accidental drops.

[__How are ratings calculated?](javascript:void\(0\))

To calculate the overall star rating and percentage breakdown by star, we
don’t use a simple average. Instead, our system considers things like how
recent a review is and if the reviewer bought the item on Amazon. It also
analyses reviews to verify trustworthiness.

### Customers say

Customers praise the phone's display quality and find it offers good value for
money. Moreover, the battery life is sufficient for heavy users, and they
appreciate its fast performance and processor capabilities. Additionally, the
camera receives positive feedback, with one customer highlighting its OIS
feature, and customers like its lightweight design that feels slim in the
hand.

 _5 out of 5 stars_

##### Perfect blend of performance and design

Absolutely Blown Away! Worth Every Penny! I’ve been using the IQOO Z10 r
,8/256 variant for a few weeks now, and it has exceeded all my expectations.
The performance is buttery smooth—even with heavy multitasking and gaming. The
display is vibrant and crisp, perfect for streaming, social media, or just
browsing. The camera setup is a total game-changer. Low light, portraits,
ultra-wide—all stunning. Battery life easily lasts a full day with heavy use,
and the fast charging is incredibly convenient. Design-wise, it looks premium
and feels solid in hand. No heating issues, no lags, just a super polished
experience all around. If you’re looking for a reliable, high-performing phone
that delivers on every front, this is it. Highly recommended!

#####  Perfect blend of performance and design

  
Reviewed in India on 4 August 2025

Absolutely Blown Away! Worth Every Penny!  
  
I’ve been using the IQOO Z10 r ,8/256 variant for a few weeks now, and it has
exceeded all my expectations. The performance is buttery smooth—even with
heavy multitasking and gaming. The display is vibrant and crisp, perfect for
streaming, social media, or just browsing.  
  
The camera setup is a total game-changer. Low light, portraits, ultra-wide—all
stunning. Battery life easily lasts a full day with heavy use, and the fast
charging is incredibly convenient.  
  
Design-wise, it looks premium and feels solid in hand. No heating issues, no
lags, just a super polished experience all around. If you’re looking for a
reliable, high-performing phone that delivers on every front, this is it.  
  
Highly recommended!
